Source Code

These source-code files were from the printout at the MIT Museum, with many thanks to Deborah Douglas, the Museum's Curator of Science and Technology, for releasing it to us. The printout was digitally photographed by Paul Fjeld. A team of volunteers transcribed the source code manually from these images or, where appropriate, modified already-transcribed but similar source Colossus 249 (Apollo 9) source code to agree with the images from the printout. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 055 OF AGC PROGRAM COMANCHE BY NASA 2021113-051
	10:28 APR.  1,1969
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

001637,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
001638,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    ERASABLE_ASSIGNMENTS.agc
001639,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     Part of the source code for Colossus 2A, AKA Comanche 055.
001640,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Command Module's (CM)
001641,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC), for Apollo 11.
001642,000007:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
001643,000008:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
001644,000009:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo.
001645,000010:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2009-05-06 RSB  Started adapting from the Colossus249/ file 
001646,000011:                                                                                                  ##                              of the same name, using Comanche055 page 
001647,000012:                                                                                                  ##                              images. Only through page 51 so far.
001648,000013:                                                                                                  ##              2009-05-07 RSB  Through page 92 so far.
001649,000014:                                                                                                  ##              2009-05-07 RSB  (Again!) First draft completed.
001650,000015:                                                                                                  ##              2009-05-20 RSB  Fixed some bugs uncovered in trial assemblies:
001651,000016:                                                                                                  ##                              EMDOT, STATEXIT, VGDISP, DVPREV, POSTCDH,
001652,000017:                                                                                                  ##                              RETROFLG not defined correctly, changed the
001653,000018:                                                                                                  ##                              typing of labels 9X9LOC1 and 9X9LOC2, 
001654,000019:                                                                                                  ##                              R32FLBIT -> R31FLBIT.
001655,000020:                                                                                                  ##              2009-05-21 RSB  Corrected definition of DELBRTMP, which 
001656,000021:                                                                                                  ##                              chained to quite a lot of off-by-one errors.
001657,000022:                                                                                                  ##                              Changed a +8 to a +8D.
001658,000023:                                                                                                  ##              2010-08-24 JL   Fixed page numbers. Added missing comment 
001659,000024:                                                                                                  ##                              character. Fixed page number comment.

001693,000058:                                                                                                  #  CONVENTIONS AND NOTATIONS UTILIZED FOR ERASABLE ASSIGNMENTS.
001694,000059: 
001695,000060:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  IS USED IN TWO WAYS.  IT IS OFTEN USED TO CHAIN A GROUP
001696,000061:                                                                                                  #                OF ASSIGNMENTS SO THAT THE GROUP MAY BE MOVED WITH THE
001697,000062:                                                                                                  #                CHANGING OF ONLY ONE CARD.  EXAMPLE.
001698,000063: 
001699,000064:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  START
001700,000065:                                                                                                  #                        Y       EQUALS  X       +SIZE.X
001701,000066:                                                                                                  #                        Z       EQUALS  Y       +SIZE.Y
001702,000067: 
001703,000068:                                                                                                  #                (X, Y, AND Z ARE CONSECUTIVE AND BEGIN AT START.       )
001704,000069:                                                                                                  #                (SIZE.X AND SIZE.Y ARE THE RESPECTIVE SIZES OF X AND Y,
001705,000070:                                                                                                  #                 USUALLY NUMERIC, IE. 1, 2, 6, 18D ETC.                )
001706,000071: 
001707,000072:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  OFTEN IMPLIES THE SHARING OF REGISTERS (DIFFERENT NAMES
001708,000073:                                                                                                  #                AND DIFFERENT DATA).  EXAMPLE.
001709,000074: 
001710,000075:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  Y
001711,000076: 
001712,000077:                                                                                                  #        =       MEANS THAT MULTIPLE NAMES HAVE BEEN GIVEN TO THE SAME DATA.
001713,000078:                                                                                                  #                (THIS IS LOGICAL EQUIVALENCE, NOT SHARING)  EXAMPLE.
001714,000079: 
001715,000080:                                                                                                  #                        X       =       Y
001716,000081: 
001717,000082:                                                                                                  #        THE SIZE AND UTILIZATION OF AN ERASABLE ARE OFTEN INCLUDED IN
001718,000083:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMENTS IN THE FOLLOWING FORM.  M(SIZE)N.
001719,000084: 
001720,000085:                                                                                                  #                M       REFERS TO THE MOBILITY OF THE ASSIGNMENT.
001721,000086:                                                                                                  #                        B       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED BY BASIC
001722,000087:                                                                                                  #                                INSTRUCTIONS AND THUS IS E-BANK SENSITIVE.
001723,000088:                                                                                                  #                        I       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED ONLY BY
001724,000089:                                                                                                  #                                INTERPRETIVE INSTRUCTIONS, AND IS THUS E-BANK
001725,000090:                                                                                                  #                                INSENSITIVE AND MAY APPEAR IN ANY E-BANK.
001726,000091: 
001727,000092:                                                                                                  #                SIZE    IS THE NUMBER OF REGISTERS INCLUDED BY THE SYMBOL.
001728,000093: 
001729,000094:                                                                                                  #                N       INDICATES THE NATURE OR PERMANENCE OF THE CONTENTS.
001730,000095:                                                                                                  #                        PL      MEANS THAT THE CONTENTS ARE PAD LOADED.
001731,000096:                                                                                                  #                        DSP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED FOR A DISPLAY.
001732,000097:                                                                                                  #                        PRM     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS PERMANENT, IE. IT
001733,000098:                                                                                                  #                                IS USED DURING THE ENTIRE MISSION FOR ONE
001734,000099:                                                                                                  #                                PURPOSE AND CANNOT BE SHARED.
001735,000100:                                                                                                  #                        TMP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED TEMPORARILY OR
001736,000101:                                                                                                  #                                IS A SCRATCH REGISTER FOR THE ROUTINE TO WHICH
001737,000102:                                                                                                  #                                IT IS ASSIGNED.  THAT IS, IT NEED NOT BE SET
001738,000103:                                                                                                  #                                PRIOR TO INVOCATION OF THE ROUTINE NOR DOES IT
001739,000104:                                                                                                  #                                CONTAIN USEFUL OUTPUT TO ANOTHER ROUTINE.  THUS

Page 38 

001741,000106:                                                                                                  #                                IT MAY BE SHARED WITH ANY OTHER ROUTINE WHICH
001742,000107:                                                                                                  #                                IS NOT ACTIVE IN PARALLEL.
001743,000108:                                                                                                  #                        IN      MEANS INPUT TO THE ROUTINE AND IT IS PROBABLY
001744,000109:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001745,000110:                                                                                                  #                        OUT     MEANS OUTPUT FROM THE ROUTINE, PROBABLY
001746,000111:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001747,000112:

001749,000114: 
001750,000115:                                                                                                  #  SPECIAL REGISTERS.
001751,000116: 
001752,000117: 37,2001                        A                  EQUALS   0                                     
001753,000118: 37,2001                        L                  EQUALS   1                                     #  L AND Q ARE BOTH CHANNELS AND REGISTERS.
001754,000119: 37,2001                        Q                  EQUALS   2                                     
001755,000120: 37,2001                        EBANK              EQUALS   3                                     
001756,000121: 37,2001                        FBANK              EQUALS   4                                     
001757,000122: 37,2001                        Z                  EQUALS   5                                     #  ADJACENT TO FBANK AND BBANK FOR DXCH Z
001758,000123: 37,2001                        BBANK              EQUALS   6                                     #  (DTCB) AND DXCH FBANK (DTCF).
001759,000124:                                                                                                  #  REGISTER 7 IS A ZERO-SOURCE, USED BY ZL.
001760,000125: 
001761,000126: 37,2001                        ARUPT              EQUALS   10                                    #  INTERRUPT STORAGE.
001762,000127: 37,2001                        LRUPT              EQUALS   11                                    
001763,000128: 37,2001                        QRUPT              EQUALS   12                                    
001764,000129: 37,2001                        SAMPTIME           EQUALS   13                                    #  SAMPLED TIME 1 & 2.
001765,000130: 37,2001                        ZRUPT              EQUALS   15                                    #  (13 AND 14 ARE SPARES.)
001766,000131: 37,2001                        BANKRUPT           EQUALS   16                                    #  USUALLY HOLDS FBANK OR BBANK.
001767,000132: 37,2001                        BRUPT              EQUALS   17                                    #  RESUME ADDRESS AS WELL.
001768,000133: 
001769,000134: 37,2001                        CYR                EQUALS   20                                    
001770,000135: 37,2001                        SR                 EQUALS   21                                    
001771,000136: 37,2001                        CYL                EQUALS   22                                    
001772,000137: 37,2001                        EDOP               EQUALS   23                                    #  EDITS INTERPRETIVE OPERATION CODE PAIRS.
001773,000138: 
001774,000139: 37,2001                        TIME2              EQUALS   24                                    
001775,000140: 37,2001                        TIME1              EQUALS   25                                    
001776,000141: 37,2001                        TIME3              EQUALS   26                                    
001777,000142: 37,2001                        TIME4              EQUALS   27                                    
001778,000143: 37,2001                        TIME5              EQUALS   30                                    
001779,000144: 37,2001                        TIME6              EQUALS   31                                    
001780,000145: 37,2001                        CDUX               EQUALS   32                                    
001781,000146: 37,2001                        CDUY               EQUALS   33                                    
001782,000147: 37,2001                        CDUZ               EQUALS   34                                    
001783,000148: 37,2001                        CDUT               EQUALS   35                                    #  OPTICS TRUNNION CDU (WAS OPTY).
001784,000149: 37,2001  0000035               OPTY               =        CDUT                                  
001785,000150: 37,2001                        CDUS               EQUALS   36                                    #  OPTICS SHAFT CDU (WAS OPTX).
001786,000151: 37,2001  0000036               OPTX               =        CDUS                                  
001787,000152: 37,2001                        PIPAX              EQUALS   37                                    
001788,000153: 37,2001                        PIPAY              EQUALS   40                                    
001789,000154: 37,2001                        PIPAZ              EQUALS   41                                    
001790,000155: 37,2001                        BMAGX              EQUALS   42                                    
001791,000156: 37,2001                        BMAGY              EQUALS   43                                    
001792,000157: 37,2001                        BMAGZ              EQUALS   44                                    
001793,000158: 37,2001                        INLINK             EQUALS   45                                    
001794,000159: 37,2001                        RNRAD              EQUALS   46                                    
001795,000160: 37,2001                        GYROCTR            EQUALS   47                                    
001796,000161: 37,2001                        GYROCMD            EQUALS   47                                    
001797,000162: 37,2001                        CDUXCMD            EQUALS   50                                    
001798,000163: 37,2001                        CDUYCMD            EQUALS   51

001804,000169: 37,2001  0000053               OPTYCMD            =        CDUTCMD
